Abstract: Automotive electronic control units (ECUs) are intricate systems with hundreds of individual functions, numerous software components, and multiple interdependent tasks. A prevalent structural pattern in these systems are so-called cause-effect chains. While significant research efforts have been dedicated to the temporal analysis and optimization of these chains, particularly minimizing data age and function response times, other crucial non-functional properties remain relatively underexplored. In particular, the safety integrity level (SIL) classification substantially influences the system design by determining task colocation strategies. Improper sharing of functions or interweaving tasks with different safety levels can compromise the integrity of critical functions. Additionally, AUTOSAR basic software (BSW) (e.g. OS, runtime environment, communication stacks, or diagnostics) introduces complexity that varies based on task characteristics and SIL categories. Furthermore, memory requirements present another critical challenge, given the diversity of memory architectures and SIL-specific dependencies that strongly constrain task allocations. This paper thoroughly characterizes a real-world automotive application, describing an automotive application based on SIL constraints, the impact of basic software, and memory requirements. In this context, the Driverator configuration framework is introduced for scalable system analysis.

### [197] [Agentic Repository Mining: A Multi-Task Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04845)
*Johannes Härtel*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究LLM代理（能通过bash命令动态探索仓库）是否能在软件仓库分类任务中媲美简单LLM（接收预工程化上下文）。实验表明代理在4项任务、8种配置和4943个分类中达到竞争性准确率，主要优势在于鲁棒性：避免上下文窗口溢出、规模不依赖工件大小。对100个分歧案例的诊断发现，规范模糊和有限上下文下的标签问题表明，针对此类真实标签的准确率可能低估了拥有更广上下文访问权限的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 人工标注软件仓库中的工件（提交、审查、代码行等）成本高且容易出错，有限的上下文常导致错误分类或标签不确定性。作者想要探索是否能让LLM代理通过动态探索仓库来替代需要预工程化上下文的简单LLM，同时保持分类质量。

Method: 作者设计了LLM代理，能够通过标准bash命令动态探索软件仓库来获取上下文，并与接收预工程化上下文的简单LLM进行对比。实验覆盖4个分类任务、8种方法配置，共4943个分类样本。此外，对100个人工与模型标签不一致的案例进行了人工诊断分析。

Result: LLM代理在分类准确率上达到与简单LLM竞争的水平；主要优势在于鲁棒性：避免上下文窗口溢出问题且能独立于工件大小进行扩展。对100个分歧案例的诊断发现，许多分歧源于标注规范模糊或标注者在有限上下文下产生的标签，说明针对此类真实标签评估可能低估了拥有更广上下文的方法的表现。

Conclusion: LLM代理可以在不依赖预工程化上下文的情况下达到有竞争力的分类质量，尤其在鲁棒性方面具有显著优势。现有的基于有限上下文的真实标签可能不足以准确评估拥有更广泛上下文访问能力的方法。

Abstract: Mining software repositories often requires classifying artifacts like commits, reviews, code lines, or entire repositories into categories. Human labeling is expensive and error-prone; limited context frequently leads to misclassifications or uncertainty in labels. We investigate whether LLM agents that dynamically explore repositories through standard bash commands can match the classification quality of simple LLMs that receive pre-engineered context. Across four tasks, eight approach configurations, and 4943 classifications, agents achieve competitive accuracy despite retrieving their own context. The primary advantage is robustness: agents avoid context-window overflows and scale independently of artifact size. A manual diagnosis of 100 cases where approaches disagree with the ground truth reveals specification ambiguities and labels produced under limited context, suggesting that accuracy against such ground truth may underestimate approaches with broader context access.

### [198] [SynConfRoute: Syntax-Aware Routing for Efficient Code Completion with Small CodeLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04894)
*Kishanthan Thangarajah,Boyuan Chen,Ahmed E. Hassan*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出SynConfRoute方法，通过结合token置信度和语法验证，在本地小模型（1B-3B）和远程大模型之间智能路由代码补全请求，在保护代码隐私的同时，将正确率提升至78.9%（超过480B大模型7.4%），并减少58%的加速器使用量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业需要在代码补全的质量和隐私之间取得平衡：小模型可在本地运行保护隐私但能力不足，大模型效果好但存在代码泄露风险且部署成本高。现有路由方法仅依赖置信度，忽略语法有效性，导致无效代码被接受。

Method: SynConfRoute是一种无需训练的方法，结合token置信度与语法验证（检查代码是否为有效语法），自动决定每个请求是使用本地小模型还是升级到大模型。该方法在29个代码LLM（0.5B-480B）上进行了系统性评估。

Result: 3B模型与32B模型性能相当（小10倍）；46%的小模型错误输出为无效代码；SynConfRoute比纯置信度路由提升6.4%（常规）和31%（多语言）；整体pipeline达到78.9%，比单独使用480B模型高7.4%，同时减少58%加速器使用；在所有三种语言上均优于置信度路由，且从不拒绝正确的本地补全。

Conclusion: 模型系列和代码专用训练比模型大小更重要；语法验证是提升代码补全路由质量的关键；SynConfRoute可直接部署（无需训练），在隐私、质量和效率之间实现有效平衡。

Abstract: Enterprises want AI code completion that is both high-quality and private, but they face a tension: proprietary models yield better results yet risk exposing proprietary code, while self-hosting large models is expensive and hard to maintain. As a lighter alternative, small CodeLLMs (1B-3B) can run on a developer's workstation accelerator with code never leaving the machine, but they fail on harder tasks. A practical solution is to use the small model for most requests and selectively route difficult ones to a larger self-hosted model. In this study, we evaluate 29 code specialized LLMs (0.5B-480B) from 12 families on execution-based fill-in-the-middle (FIM) code completion benchmarks across Python, Java, and C++, and find that model family and code specialized training matter more than size: a 3B model matches a 32B model despite being 10x smaller. Analyzing the 3B model's failures, we discover that 46% of its incorrect completions are not valid code. To enable efficient code completion, we propose SynConfRoute, a training-free method that combines token confidence with syntax validation to automatically decide per-request whether to keep the local completion or escalate to a larger self-hosted model. SynConfRoute improves pass@1 by 6.4% over confidence only routing on routine completions and by up to 31% on harder multi-language tasks, and the resulting pipeline achieves 78.9% on routine completions, 7.4% higher than always using the 480B model alone, while reducing accelerator usage by 58%. SynConfRoute generalizes across Python, Java, and C++, improving over confidence only routing on all three languages without ever rejecting a correct local completion. The pipeline uses off-the-shelf models with no custom training, making it immediately deployable in practice.

</details>


### [199] [Conflict Essences for Transformation Rules with Nested Application Conditions -- Long Version](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04947)
*Alexander Lauer,Jens Kosiol,Leen Lambers,Gabriele Taentzer*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文扩展了禁用本质（disabling essences）的概念，支持任意嵌套条件（不仅是交替量化范式），并引入符号冲突本质（symbolic conflict essences）来捕捉两个图变换规则间的交互，证明变换对并行依赖当且仅当符号冲突本质可嵌入其中，并在粘性HLR范畴中给出结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的冲突/依赖分析依赖关键对和初始冲突，但冲突信息实际包含在更小的结构中（禁用/冲突本质）。已有工作只支持交替量化范式（AQNF）的条件，缺乏对任意嵌套条件的支持。

Method: 将禁用本质从支持AQNF条件扩展到支持任意嵌套条件；基于禁用本质构造（符号）冲突本质；在粘性HLR范畴（含多种图结构）中形式化证明冲突本质与并行依赖的等价关系。

Result: 变换对是并行依赖的当且仅当符号冲突本质可嵌入其中；符号冲突本质与带应用条件的变换规则的初始冲突相关联。

Conclusion: 提出的符号冲突本质为图变换规则的冲突分析提供了更紧凑、更通用的形式化基础，适用于更广泛的应用条件类型和图结构。

Abstract: Conflict and dependency analysis is an important static analysis tool that provides an overview of the potential interactions of (graph) transformation rules. This analysis is based on critical pairs and initial conflicts, which represent conflicting transformations in a minimal context. However, the crucial information about a conflicting transformation pair is contained in much smaller structures, called disabling/conflict essences in existing research. Recently, we introduced disabling essences for rules with application conditions which contain the information on how an application condition can be violated by another rule. In this paper, we extend the notion of disabling essences to support not only application conditions in Alternating Quantifier Normal Form, but also arbitrary nested conditions. We introduce (symbolic) conflict essences that are constructed from disabling essences and which capture the interaction between two rules. We show that a transformation pair is parallel dependent if and only if a symbolic conflict essence can be embedded into it and relate symbolic conflict essences to initial conflicts for transformation rules with application conditions. We present our results for adhesive HLR categories, which includes several types of graph-like structures.

</details>

### [201] [OpenCLAW-Nexus: A Self-Reinforcing Trust Framework for Byzantine-Resilient Decentralized Federated Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04091)
*Wenyang Jia,Qiankang Xu,Ziwei Yan,Chunhua Kang,Yang Yang,Jinglu He,Kai Lei*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 提出OpenCLAW-Nexus框架，通过折扣Beta声誉模型统一节点选择、聚合（Rep-FedAvg）和BFT共识，解决去中心化联邦学习中的信任缺口问题。在1000节点全球测试中，非IID CIFAR-10数据集下含20%拜占庭节点时达到72.6%准确率，300节点女巫攻击下保持84.2%验证正确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 去中心化联邦学习(DFL)消除了中央聚合器但带来了严重的信任缺口：缺乏可信协调者时系统易受拜占庭攻击和女巫攻击，而现有方案将节点选择、聚合和共识视为孤立模块，且常依赖真实数据集——这在真正的去中心化环境中不可用。

Method: 提出OpenCLAW-Nexus自强化信任框架，核心是折扣Beta声誉模型，统一三个功能：(1)基于声誉的节点选择，(2)声誉加权聚合Rep-FedAvg（无需真实数据集），(3)声誉感知的BFT共识。理论上证明了非IID数据和带噪声评估下诚实节点与拜占庭节点的声誉可分性。

Result: 全球测试（3个云提供商、9个区域、1000节点）：(1)非IID CIFAR-10+20%拜占庭节点→Rep-FedAvg达72.6%准确率，差分隐私达记录级水平，距集中式FLTrust仅差0.5个百分点；(2)300节点女巫攻击→声誉加权共识保持84.2%验证正确性，而PoW为62.8%、PoS为47.6%。

Conclusion: OpenCLAW-Nexus通过单一声誉原语统一了DFL的三个关键环节，无需可信数据集即可有效防御拜占庭和女巫攻击，性能接近集中式方法，优于传统PoW/PoS共识机制。

Abstract: Decentralized Federated Learning (DFL) eliminates the central aggregator but introduces a severe 'trust gap': without a trusted coordinator, the system becomes vulnerable to Byzantine and Sybil attacks, while existing solutions treat node selection, aggregation, and consensus as isolated modules, often relying on a trusted root dataset unavailable in truly decentralized settings.We propose OpenCLAW-Nexus, a self-reinforcing trust framework that bridges this gap through a single primitive, a discounted Beta-reputation model, that unifies reputation-based node selection, reputation-weighted aggregation Rep-FedAvg, and reputation-aware BFT consensus. Rep-FedAvg eliminates the trusted root dataset requirement; we formally prove reputation separation between honest and Byzantine nodes under non-IID data with noisy evaluations.On a 1,000-node global testbed spanning three cloud providers and nine regions, Rep-FedAvg achieves 72.6% accuracy on non-IID CIFAR-10 with 20% Byzantine nodes and record-level differential privacy, within 0.5,pp of centralized FLTrust.Under a 300-node Sybil attack, reputation-weighted consensus maintains 84.2% validation correctness versus 62.8% (PoW) and 47.6% (PoS).

</details>


### [202] [Resilient AI Supercomputer Networking using MRC and SRv6](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04333)
*Joao Araujo,Alex Chow,Mark Handley,Ryder Lewis,Christoph Paasch,Jitendra Padhye,Michael Papamichael,Greg Steinbrecher,Amin Tootoonchian,Lihua Yuan,S. Anantharamu,Abhishek Dosi,Mohit Garg,Mahdieh Ghazi,Torsten Hoefler,Deepal Jayasinghe,Jithin Jose,Abdul Kabbani,Guohan Lu,Yang Wang,K. Doddapaneni,Murali Garimella,Vipin Jain,Yanfang Le,H. Nagulapalli,S. Narayanan,Rong Pan,Rathina Sabesan,Raghava Sivaramu,Rip Sohan,Eric Davis,Dragos Dumitrescu,Mohan Kalkunte,Bhaswar Mitra,Guglielmo Morandin,Adrian Popa,Costin Raiciu,Eric Spada,John Spillane,Niranjan Vaidya,Aviv Barnea,Idan Burstein,Elazar Cohen,Yamin Friedman,Noam Katz,Masoud Moshref,Yuval Shpigelman,Shahaf Shuler,Shy Shyman,Sayantan Sur*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出三管齐下的网络优化方案（MRC传输协议+多平面Clos拓扑+静态SRv6源路由），显著降低大规模同步预训练任务的尾延迟，并在OpenAI和微软的超大规模训练集群中成功部署，用于训练前沿模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模同步预训练作业中，尾延迟（tail latency）严重制约性能，传统网络方案无法有效解决流冲突和故障恢复问题。

Method: (1) 基于RDMA的新型传输协议MRC，通过多路径喷洒和主动负载均衡消除流冲突；(2) 采用多平面Clos拓扑，利用高交换机端口密度和冗余性构建超10万GPU的两层训练集群；(3) 使用SRv6实现静态源路由，使MRC能自主绕过故障。

Result: 在OpenAI和微软最大规模训练集群中部署，成功用于训练最新前沿模型，显著降低尾延迟，使AI训练任务能承受大量此前会导致训练中断的网络故障。

Conclusion: 所提出的三管齐下方案有效解决了大规模分布式训练中的网络瓶颈，提升了训练稳定性和效率，是支撑超大规模AI训练的关键基础设施技术。

Abstract: Tail latency dominates the performance of synchronous pretraining jobs when running at very large scales. We describe a three-pronged approach: (1) a new RDMA-based transport protocol, MRC, sprays across many paths and actively load-balances between them, eliminating the issue of flow collisions (2) the use of multi-plane Clos topologies to get the benefits of high switch radix and redundancy, allowing training clusters well over 100K GPUs to be built as two-tier topologies while increasing physical redundancy, and (3) the use of static source-routing using SRv6 to allow MRC the freedom to bypass failures by itself. We describe our experiences running MRC and static SRv6 routing in production in OpenAI and Microsoft's largest training clusters, where it has been used to train the latest frontier models. We demonstrate how MRC allows AI training jobs to ride out many network failures that previously would have interrupted training.

### [203] [Worst-Case Discovery and Runtime Protection for RL-Based Network Controllers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04373)
*Hongyu Hè,Minhao Jin,Maria Apostolaki*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: ReGuard是一个框架，能够发现RL网络控制器在最坏情况下的性能差距，并通过轻量级规则在推理时提供保护，无需重新训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RL控制器在网络任务中平均性能良好，但在某些网络条件下性能会严重下降，而枚举验证和形式化验证方法均不可行，因此需要一种发现并防护最坏情况的方法。

Method: 将发现最坏情况场景建模为双层遗憾最大化问题，获得性能差距的认证下界；将发现的轨迹作为反事实分析，编译为轻量级逻辑规则，在推理时检测风险状态并进行干预。

Result: 在Pensieve、Sage、Park三个RL网络控制器上，ReGuard发现性能差距达43-64%，比最强基线大57%到6倍；通过规则防护将差距缩小79-85%，且不影响正常性能。

Conclusion: ReGuard不仅能有效发现并缩小RL控制器的最坏情况性能差距，其防护还能泛化到未发现的场景，在更广泛的网络条件下提升性能。

Abstract: RL-based controllers achieve strong average-case performance in networking tasks such as congestion control and adaptive bitrate streaming. Yet their performance can degrade severely under network conditions where strong performance is still achievable. Identifying such conditions and quantifying the resulting performance gap is intractable by enumeration, while the sequential and closed-loop nature of RL controllers makes formal verification methods impractical.
  We present ReGuard, a framework that discovers worst-case scenarios for a given RL controller and protects it against them at inference time without retraining. Discovery is formulated as a bilevel regret-maximization problem, which yields a certified lower bound on the worst-case performance gap. The discovered trajectories are then analyzed as counterfactuals and compiled into lightweight logic rules that intervene only when a risky state is detected, leaving the controller's behavior unchanged otherwise.
  We evaluate ReGuard across three RL-based network controllers: Pensieve, Sage, and Park. ReGuard discovers scenarios in which the controller's performance is 43$-$64% worse than what is achievable. ReGuard not only discovers gaps 57% to 6$\times$ larger than those found by the strongest baselines but also shrinks them by 79$-$85% via lightweight rule-based protection while preserving nominal performance. ReGuard's protection extends beyond the scenarios it discovers, improving performance across a wider range of network conditions.

</details>


### [204] [Joint Optimization of Trajectory Control, Resource Allocation, and Task Offloading for Multi-UAV-Assisted IoV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04436)
*Maoxin Ji,Qiong Wu,Pingyi Fan,Cui Zhang,Nan Cheng,Wen Chen,Khaled B. Letaief*

TL;DR: 本文针对城市密集环境下多无人机基站辅助的车联网任务卸载系统，提出了分层执行框架。通过SOCP优化无人机3D轨迹、DRL+LLM混合资源调度及线性规划确定卸载比例，显著提升了任务成功率与系统效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市密集环境中多无人机辅助车联网任务卸载面临严格的耦合约束，现有方法在系统延迟和能耗方面存在瓶颈，亟需高效的协同优化方案。

Method: 将非凸优化问题解耦为分层框架：(1) 基于SOCP的顺序分布式优化算法优化无人机3D轨迹；(2) DRL+LLM混合调度范式，DRL决定初始资源分配，LLM作为语义宏调度器修正长尾分配失衡，并引入奖励解耦机制确保策略收敛；(3) 交替优化中通过线性规划确定任务卸载比例。

Result: 仿真结果表明，所提方法在任务成功率和系统效率上显著优于传统多智能体强化学习基线方法。

Conclusion: DRL+LLM混合调度结合奖励解耦机制能有效解决多无人机协同任务卸载问题，为车联网提供了一种高效可行的解决方案。

Abstract: This paper investigates a multi-Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) joint base station-assisted Internet of Vehicles (IoV) task offloading system in dense urban environments. To minimize system delay and energy consumption under strict coupling constraints, the complex non-convex optimization problem is decoupled into a hierarchical execution framework. First, a sequential distributed optimization algorithm based on Second-Order Cone Programming (SOCP) is proposed to optimize the 3D flight trajectory of each UAV, ensuring adaptive network coverage. Second, a novel hybrid resource scheduling paradigm synergizing Deep Reinforcement Learning (DRL) and Large Language Models (LLMs) is developed. Within this framework, the DRL agent dictates the initial resource allocation, while the LLM acts as a semantic macro-scheduler to rectify long-tail allocation imbalances for failed and surplus tasks. Crucially, a reward decoupling mechanism is introduced to isolate DRL training from external LLM interventions, thereby ensuring policy convergence. Finally, the task offloading ratios are precisely determined via Linear Programming (LP) within an alternating optimization loop. Simulation results demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms traditional multi-agent reinforcement learning baselines in terms of task success rate and system efficiency.

### [205] [Queue-Aware and Resilient Routing in LEO Satellite Networks Using Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04448)
*Mudassar Liaq,Mahyar Tajeri,Peng Hu*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于队列感知的多智能体深度强化学习（MA-DRL）框架，用于解决低轨卫星网络中的动态路由问题。每个卫星作为独立智能体做本地路由决策，实现了分布式可扩展的方案。实验表明，该方法在计算开销、队列管理、鲁棒性和可扩展性方面优于Dijkstra和SARSA算法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LEO卫星网络面临高度动态拓扑、时变流量和链路故障等挑战，传统路由算法（假设静态链路度量、忽略队列积压和实时变化）在此环境中效果不佳，亟需一种能够适应动态变化、具备鲁棒性和可扩展性的路由方案。

Method: 提出队列感知的多智能体深度强化学习（MA-DRL）框架：每个卫星建模为独立智能体，负责本地路由决策；构建延迟感知优化问题，融合背景流量、卫星队列动态及弹性评分（resilience score）以增强鲁棒性。

Result: 与SARSA和Dijkstra对比：Dijkstra在理想条件下延迟最低，但计算和信令开销大（重新计算间隔5s时，本文方法开销约为Dijkstra的50%）；本文方法在队列积压管理、弹性评分和可扩展性方面表现更优，同时保持有竞争力的延迟。

Conclusion: 所提MA-DRL框架在LEO卫星网络中展现出增强的鲁棒性和可扩展性，能有效管理队列积压和应对链路故障，是一种优于传统算法的分布式路由解决方案。

Abstract: With the rapid growth in data demand and stringent latency requirements of modern applications has driven significant interest in Low Earth Orbit (LEO) satellite constellations as an emerging solution for global Internet coverage. However, routing in LEO networks remains a fundamental challenge due to highly dynamic topologies, time-varying traffic conditions, and its susceptibility to link failures. Conventional routing algorithms typically assume static link metrics and fail to account for queue backlogs or real-time system variations, making them less effective in such environments. We propose a queue-aware multi-agent deep reinforcement learning (MA-DRL) framework for routing in LEO satellite networks. Each satellite is modeled as an independent agent responsible for making local routing decisions, enabling a distributed and scalable solution. The proposed framework formulates a latency-aware optimization problem that incorporates background traffic, queue dynamics at each satellite, and a resilience score to improve robustness. We evaluate the proposed approach against the state-action-reward-state-action (SARSA) and Dijkstra algorithms. While Dijkstra achieves the lowest end-to-end latency under ideal conditions, its computational and signaling overhead becomes a significant bottleneck as the network scales. In contrast, our proposed approach incurs significantly lower overhead (approximately 50% of Dijkstra at a 5 s recalculation interval), scales efficiently with network size, and effectively manages queue backlogs and resilience under increasing traffic load, demonstrating enhanced robustness and scalability in LEO satellite networks while maintaining competitive latency and resilience scores.

</details>


### [206] [SADE: Symptom-Aware Diagnostic Escalation for LLM-Based Network Troubleshooting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04530)
*Kuan-Hao Tseng,Niruth Bogahawatta,Yasod Ginige,Kosta Dekic,Arunan Sivanathan,Suranga Seneviratne*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: SADE是一个将经典思科故障排查方法论编码为显式策略的智能体，通过分阶段诊断工作流分离证据收集与假设承诺，在NIKA基准测试中将根因定位F1分数提升37个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体在网络故障根因定位上远未达到实际部署阈值，因为它们没有编码人类网络工程师使用的分层方法论，而是依赖自由形式的推理，将证据获取与假设承诺混为一谈。

Method: SADE编码经典思科故障排查方法论为显式策略，包含：(1) 分阶段诊断工作流，分离证据获取与假设承诺；(2) 路由式故障族技能库；(3) 高效诊断辅助工具。

Result: 在523个NIKA基准测试样本（覆盖11种未见场景）上，SADE相比ReAct+GPT-5基线将根因F1提升37个百分点；控制实验表明，其中22个百分点归因于诊断策略本身，而非模型升级的副作用。

Conclusion: 显式编码领域专家的结构化方法论能显著提升LLM智能体在复杂诊断任务上的性能，且效果独立于底层模型的能力提升。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents are increasingly applied to network troubleshooting, but root-cause localization on public benchmarks remains well below practical deployment thresholds. We argue this is because existing agents do not encode the disciplined, layer-by-layer methodology that human network engineers use, and instead rely on free-form deliberation that conflates evidence acquisition with hypothesis commitment. We present SADE (Symptom-Aware Diagnostic Escalation), an agent that encodes the classical Cisco troubleshooting methodology as an explicit policy. SADE pairs a phase-gated diagnostic workflow, which separates evidence acquisition from hypothesis commitment, with a routed library of fault-family skills and high-yield diagnostic helpers. On a held-out 523 incident set of the public NIKA benchmark covering eleven unseen scenarios, SADE improves root-cause F1 by 37 percentage points over a ReAct + GPT-5 baseline; a model-controlled comparison against the same Claude Sonnet backend without the SADE policy attributes 22 of those points to the diagnostic policy alone, showing that the gain is not a side-effect of the model upgrade.

### [207] [A Separation Between Optimal Demand-Oblivious and Demand-Aware Network Throughput](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04699)
*Matthias Bentert,Chen Avin,Stefan Schmid*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文研究了需求感知网络的吞吐量问题，区分了两种吞吐量定义（经典吞吐量和弱吞吐量）和两种路由模型（直接路由和一般多跳路由），主要结论是需求感知拓扑在经典吞吐量上可达到至少5/8，优于需求 oblivious 拓扑的约1/2；同时证明了计算弱吞吐量是NP难的，而直接吞吐量可在多项式时间内求解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管需求 oblivious 吞吐量已得到广泛研究，但需求感知吞吐量（即网络拓扑可根据通信需求进行优化）的边界和计算复杂度仍知之甚少，这限制了可重构光网络等新兴技术的性能理解与优化。

Method: 系统性地研究了四种需求感知吞吐量变体：2种吞吐量定义（经典吞吐量与弱吞吐量）× 2种路由模型（直接单跳与一般多跳），分别推导了理论边界并分析了计算复杂度。

Result: 1) 需求感知拓扑的经典吞吐量渐近可达至少5/8，而需求 oblivious 吞吐量为n/(2n-1)≈1/2，证明需求感知拓扑在最坏情况下也能超越 oblivious 拓扑。2) 计算需求感知弱吞吐量是NP难的，而计算直接路由下的弱/经典吞吐量是多项式时间可解的。

Conclusion: 该工作解决了文献中关于经典吞吐量的开放问题，揭示了需求感知拓扑的理论优势，并刻画了相关优化问题的计算复杂性边界。

Abstract: The performance of distributed applications often critically depends on the interconnecting network or more specifically on its throughput: how fast data can be carried across a network. Over the last years, great progress has been made in understanding demand-oblivious throughput: how fast a given demand matrix describing pairwise communication requirements can be served on a given network. However, surprisingly little is known today about the achievable demand-aware throughput: the throughput on a network topology which can be optimized toward the demand. Such demand-aware networks have recently gained popularity in datacenters and are enabled by emerging reconfigurable optical technologies.
  In this paper, we are interested in both the achievable demand-aware throughput bounds as well as in the computational complexity of finding a throughput-optimizing network topology. We take a systematic approach and investigate four variants of demand-aware throughput: we analyze, and derive bounds for, two definitions of throughput, the classic throughput usually considered in the literature, and a new generalized definition which we call weak throughput; for each of them, we consider two routing models, a direct one, where demand can only be served on a single hop, and a general one, where multi-hop routing is allowed.
  Our main result is a separation result which solves an open problem in the literature about the classic throughput definition, showing that demand-aware topologies can outperform demand-oblivious topologies even in the worst case: the demand-aware throughput asymptotically approaches at least 5/8, while it is known that the demand-oblivious throughput is n/(2n-1), which is roughly 1/2. In terms of computational complexity, we show that computing the demand-aware weak throughput is NP-hard, but computing the demand-aware (weak) direct throughput is polynomial-time solvable.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在卫星通信中，尺寸、重量和功耗（SWaP）约束极为严格，亟需透明全光交换技术提升资源利用效率。不同交换范式的选择直接影响地面站流量组装和路径计算算法设计，进而决定星上交换结构的具体需求。

Method: 本文对比了多种光交换技术（MEMS、集成光子学等），从交换速度、功耗、插入损耗等维度评估性能，并基于最大可调度流量块大小进行仿真分析。

Abstract: To enable efficient resource utilization under stringent Size, Weight, and Power (SWaP) constraints through transparent and all-optical switched satellites transmission, various switching paradigms can be considered, including packet, burst, or circuit. To this end, the traffic assembly and algorithmic design for path computations at the ground stations play a key role in determining the switching fabric design. Generally, traffic can be buffered and assembled in chunks at the ground stations and forwarded over the pre-computed optical path in space, similar to terrestrial optical burst switching or fast circuit switching. Regardless of the chosen paradigm, the switching fabric must satisfy specific latency performance requirements. This paper studies the performance of all-optical satellite networks based on the maximum traffic chunk sizes that can be scheduled and the performance of optical switching fabrics in the future over all-optical constellations. We consider various optical switching technologies, including MEMS- and integrated photonic-based solutions, in the context of switching speed, power consumption, and insertion loss. Simulation results indicate that traffic chunk size critically impacts the performance required by optical switching fabrics onboard a satellite.

### [209] [Look Once, Beam Twice: Camera-Primed Real-Time Double-Directional mmWave Beam Management for Vehicular Connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05071)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 毫米波V2X通信面临严重路径损耗和移动导致的波束未对准问题，现有方法训练开销大且泛化能力差，需要快速、双方向的波束对齐方法。

Method: VIBE融合机器学习、模型推理和闭环RF反馈，利用摄像头观测缩小波束搜索空间，结合轻量级波束精调与偏移跟踪机制，实现混合模型驱动的闭环学习架构。

Result: 在室内外测试平台、公开数据集和实时车载实验中，VIBE展示强泛化能力；中断率低至1.1-1.4%，优于5G NR层次化波束赋形和端到端ML模型。

Conclusion: 混合模型驱动的闭环学习架构比端到端训练的ML模型更适合实际毫米波车载通信，且代码已开源。

Abstract: Millimeter-wave (mmWave) frequencies promise multi-gigabit connectivity for vehicle-to-everything (V2X) networks, but face challenges in terms of severe path loss and mobility-related beam misalignment. Reliable V2X connectivity requires fast, double-directional beam alignment. However, existing methods suffer from high training overhead and limited generalization to unseen scenarios. This paper presents VIsion-based BEamforming(VIBE), a hybrid model-based, closed-loop, learning architecture for real-time double-directional mmWave beam management primed by camera sensing. VIBE fuses machine learning, model-based reasoning, and closed-loop RF feedback to balance beam-pair establishment latency with link quality. VIBE bypasses exhaustive training overhead and accelerates link establishment by leveraging camera observations to reduce the beam-search space. Lightweight beam refinement and offset tracking mechanisms adaptively refine beams in response to dynamic application requirements. VIBE is implemented and evaluated across online indoor/outdoor testbeds, public datasets, and real-time vehicular experiments, demonstrating strong generalization capabilities, making it suitable for real-time V2X communication. Comparisons with 5G NR hierarchical beamforming show that VIBE consistently maintains lower outage rates. Furthermore, VIBE outperforms state-of-the-art end-to-end ML models for beam selection when evaluated on public datasets and achieves outage rates as low as 1.1-1.4 %. The results show that a hybrid model-based, closed-loop learning architecture is better suited for real-world mmWave vehicular connectivity than end-to-end trained ML models. For reproducibility, we publish our code to https://github.com/UNL-CPN-Lab/Look-Once-Beam-Twice.

### [210] [SILC: Lookahead Caching for Short-form Video Delivery Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.05188)
*Maleeha Masood,Shreya Kannan,Om Chabra,Deepak Vasisht,Indranil Gupta*

Main category: cs.NI

TL;DR: 本文提出SILC——一种基于推送推荐系统和流行度帕累托分布的短视频缓存系统，通过利用对未来请求的可预见性，相比10种最先进缓存策略，可降低CDN中间带宽成本11.1%-111%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 短视频平台（TikTok、Instagram Reels、YouTube Shorts）占据日益增长的互联网流量，但现有CDN缓存系统未充分利用两个独特机会：(1) 推送式推荐系统可预知即将到来的请求；(2) 视频流行度呈高度偏斜的帕累托分布，导致时空重叠。现有缓存策略未利用这些特性优化短视频分发。

Method: 设计SILC缓存系统，利用推送式推荐系统的请求可见性（lookahead-aware）和视频流行度分布特征。通过真实用户追踪（含100名全球TikTok用户数据捐赠和线下实验）模拟10000名并发用户的流量，与10种SOTA缓存淘汰策略（包括启发式和基于学习的）进行对比评估。

Result: 相比10种SOTA缓存策略，SILC降低CDN中间带宽成本11.1%至111%，同时降低缓存未命中率。

Conclusion: SILC证明了利用短视频推荐系统可预见性和流行度分布特性可显著提升CDN缓存效率，为短视频平台的基础设施优化提供了新思路。

Abstract: Short video platforms like TikTok, Instagram Reels, and YouTube Shorts have gained immense popularity in the last few years and are responsible for a large and growing fraction of Internet traffic. We identify two unique opportunities for improving short video delivery using their existing interactions with content delivery networks (CDNs). First, short videos use a push-based recommendation system, where the user is presented a sequence of videos recommended by the algorithm rather than user explicitly picking content to watch (e.g., in YouTube). Such push-based short video systems offer a unique opportunity for system design by providing visibility into upcoming requests. Second, the popularity of these videos follows a highly skewed Pareto distribution, leading to geographical and temporal overlap amongst videos being served. We leverage these opportunities to build SILC - a lookahead-aware caching system, aimed at (i) reducing CDN cache miss rates, as well as (ii) reducing midgress bandwidth between the CDN and the origin server. Our evaluation of SILC uses traces that we collect from real users, through (i) an in-person user study, and (ii) a data donation program involving 100 TikTok users across the world. Using a combination of these traces, we simulate traffic from 10,000 simultaneous users. Our evaluation shows that, compared to 10 state-of-the-art heuristic and learning-based cache eviction policies, SILC reduces a CDN's midgress costs by 11.1% to 111%.

</details>

### [211] [Reddit's Globalization over Twenty Years: Inferring Community Time Zone from Activity Timestamps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.04371)
*Franco Della Negra,Mattia Samory,Matteo Cinelli*

Main category: cs.SI

TL;DR: 本文提出并验证了仅通过每小时活动计数推断在线社区时区的方法。研究发现，简单的"凌晨4点活动最低"启发式方法几乎与复杂方法精度相当（误差在一小时内），在Reddit上最佳方法可达30分钟精度。该方法具有跨平台可移植性，无需用户披露信息，适用于研究在线行为的地理结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在线社区是全球性现象，但评估其实际地理分布需要准确且可扩展的测量方法。现有方法存在局限，因此需要一种简单、准确且无需用户隐私数据的地理位置推断方法。

Method: 基于"发帖节奏编码昼夜节律"的已知发现，比较了时域方法和频域方法的性能，并提出一个简约启发式：活动量在当地时间凌晨4点左右达到最低点。在Reddit上验证了方法的准确性、所需数据量、泛化能力，并大规模应用于Reddit的地理演变分析。

Result: 最佳方法精度达30分钟以内，不到1000条评论即可达到最佳性能。简单启发式方法平均误差在一小时以内，且与Reddit实际地理分布显著相关。该方法在不同文化主题社区（体育、金融等）中均具有泛化能力。

Conclusion: 基于活动模式的时区推断方法简单有效，可作为任何研究在线行为地理结构时的实用基线方法。具有跨平台可移植性，无需用户数据披露。

Abstract: Online communities are a global phenomenon, but assessing their actual geographical spread requires accurate and scalable measurement. We propose and evaluate methods that infer the time zone of online communities solely from their temporal activity patterns, requiring nothing beyond hourly activity counts. Grounding our approach in the well-established finding that posting rhythms encode circadian structure, we compare time-domain and frequency-domain methods against a parsimonious heuristic: that activity reaches its minimum around 4 a.m. local time. On Reddit, we show that the best-performing method is accurate to a sub-30-minute resolution, and that fewer than a thousand comments are sufficient to reach peak performance. Similarly, our heuristic almost matches the accuracy of more complex methods, recovering the correct time zone within a one-hour margin on average. This simple method correlates significantly with the actual distribution of Reddit's geographical spread; we validate its generalizability across communities organized around diverse cultural phenomena, from sports to finance, and apply it at scale to characterize the geographic evolution of Reddit from its founding to the present. Our method is portable across platforms and requires no user disclosure, making it a practical baseline for any study that must account for the geographic structure of online behavior.

</details>
